FILL_ALL_LIST_PRC
Select FLG_SR||'-'||FLG_DESC,to_char(FLG_VALUE)
        From S_Flags      
        Where FLG_CODE='RCPT_PAY_TYPE_NAME_POS'
         And Flg_value in(1,4)
         And LANG_NO=
         AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM S_FLAGS_PRIV
                 WHERE U_ID=
                   AND FLG_CODE=S_FLAGS.FLG_CODE
                   AND FLG_VALUE=S_FLAGS.FLG_VALUE
                   AND PRIV_FLAG=1)
        Order By  FLG_SR

,1,Nvl(So_A_Name,So_E_Name),Nvl(So_E_Name,So_A_Name)),To_Char(So_Type)
				From Ias_Sorder_Types
				Where ((
=1) Or Exists(Select S_Type From Ias_Priv_Ar
				Where U_Id=
				  And Nvl(Add_Flag,0)=1 
				  And Ias_Priv_Ar.S_Type=Ias_Sorder_Types.So_Type
          And Ias_Priv_Ar.Ar_Type=2  
				  And Rownum<=1))
				Order By So_Type

DYNAMIC_LOV_ITM_AVL_QTY
 SELECT I_CODE,Decode(
,1,Nvl(I_Name,I_E_Name),Nvl(I_E_Name,I_Name)) I_Name,itm_unt,W_Code,Expire_Date,Batch_No,ITM_QTY
	    FROM (
	    Select A.I_Code,A.W_Code,Decode(Expire_Date,'01/01/1900','',Expire_Date) Expire_Date,
	               Decode(Batch_No, '0','', Batch_No) Batch_No,A.Avl_Qty ITM_QTY
	              From IAS_ITM_MST M,IAS_ITM_DTL D,MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY A
	              WHERE M.I_CODE=D.I_CODE
	              AND D.I_CODE=A.I_CODE 
	              AND Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
 And I_Code=
 And W_Code=
 Order By I_Code,w_code

CHK_SALE_PRICE_PRC
QUERY
SELECT I_PRICE   FROM IAS_ITEM_PRICE,IAS_PRICING_LEVELS  WHERE IAS_ITEM_PRICE.I_CODE = :b1  AND IAS_ITEM_PRICE.ITM_UNT = :b2  AND IAS_ITEM_PRICE.LEV_NO = IAS_PRICING_LEVELS.LEV_NO  AND ROUND(NVL(IAS_ITEM_PRICE.I_PRICE,0) * NVL(IAS_GEN_PKG.GET_CUR_RATE(IAS_PRICING_LEVELS.A_CY),1) ) = ROUND(:b3)  AND NVL(INACTIVE,0) != 1  AND ROWNUM <= 1"

SELECT NULL "FLD1", NULL "FLD2", NULL "FLD3", NULL "FLD4", NULL "FLD5", NULL "FLD6", NULL "FLD7", NULL "FLD8", NULL "FLD9", NULL "FLD10", NULL "FLD11" , NULL "FLD12", NULL "FLD13" , NULL "FLD14" , NULL "FLD15",

RG_C_CODE
Select customer.c_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_a_name, c_e_name),
                Nvl (c_e_name, c_a_name)) c_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_group_a_name, c_group_e_name),
                Nvl (c_group_e_name, c_group_a_name)) group_name,
       customer.c_a_code a_code
  From customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     customer.c_Group_Code = Customer_Group.c_Group_Code(+) 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = customer.c_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And c_code = customer.c_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
And  customer.c_code Like  Decode(:SALES_ORDER.c_code,Null,'%',:SALES_ORDER.c_code||'%') 
And Nvl(customer.Inactive,0)=0
Order By c_code
C_CODE
C_NAME
GROUP_NAME
A_CODE
RG_C_CODE_ADVNC_PYMNT
Select customer.c_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_a_name, c_e_name),
                Nvl (c_e_name, c_a_name)) c_name,       
       customer.c_a_code a_code,
       IAS_CST_ACCNT.a_code a_code_advnc_pymnt
  From customer,IAS_CST_ACCNT
 Where 
     customer.C_CODE = IAS_CST_ACCNT.C_CODE(+) 
     AND IAS_CST_ACCNT.AC_TYP(+)=3
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = customer.c_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And c_code = customer.c_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
And  customer.c_code Like  Decode(:SALES_ORDER.c_code,Null,'%',:SALES_ORDER.c_code||'%') 
And Nvl(customer.Inactive,0)=0
Order By customer.c_code

RG_I_CODE
select m.i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,d.itm_unt unit,m.i_desc ,A.I_PRICE,M.VNDR_I_CODE
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D ,IAS_ITEM_PRICE A
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
and Nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0 and Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0 
AND NVL(M.USE_BATCH_NO,0)=0 
AND M.I_CODE=A.I_CODE
AND D.ITM_UNT=A.ITM_UNT
And  Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,A.W_Code,5,A.Brn_No,1) 
               = Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,:Parameter.Def_Wcode,5,:Parameter.Def_Brn_No,1)
AND A.LEV_NO=:Parameter.Price_Level
AND NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0))
AND NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0)=0
And Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(m.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, upper(M.I_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_E_Name),
                3,upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code,' ','%'),:ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code) || '%')
order by Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,i_name,i_e_name),m.i_code

Select   D.Itm_Unt,
         Lvl_Unit,
 Round(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Itm_Price_Docacy(M.I_Code,
                                         D.Itm_Unt,
                                                :SALES_ORDER.ORDER_CUR,
                                                :Parameter.Local_Cur,
                                                :Parameter.Stk_Cur,                                                     :SALES_ORDER.CUR_RATE,
                                                :Parameter.STOCK_RATE,
                                                :Parameter.Price_Level,
                                                 :Parameter.Def_Wcode,
                                                 null,
                                                 1,
                                                 :Parameter.Price_Type),2) I_Price,
         P_Size
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And D.I_Code = :ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0
     And Nvl(D.INACTIVE,0)=0
and Exists (select 1 from IAS_ITEM_PRICE
 where i_code=m.i_code and Itm_Unt=D.Itm_Unt and nvl(I_PRICE,0)>0 and RowNum<=1)
Order By Lvl_Unit

         Lvl_Unit, 
         D.P_Size

     And Nvl(D.INACTIVE,0)=0
Order By d.Lvl_Unit

RG_I_PRICE
Select Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Lev_A_Name, Lev_E_Name), Nvl (Lev_E_Name, Lev_A_Name)) L_Name,
       A_Cy,  
       I_Price, 
       Round(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Itm_Price_Docacy (:ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code, 
                                  :ORDER_DETAIL.Itm_Unt, 
                                  :SALES_ORDER.ORDER_CUR,
                                  :Parameter.Local_Cur,
                                  :Parameter.Stk_Cur,
                                  :SALES_ORDER.cur_Rate,                                
                                  :Parameter.Stock_Rate,
                                  Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No),2) Sale_Price
  From Ias_Item_Price, Ias_Pricing_Levels
 Where Ias_Item_Price.I_Code = :ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code
   And Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No = Ias_Pricing_Levels.Lev_No
   And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1 ) 
         Or (Exists (
          Select Lev_No
            From Ias_Priv_Price
           Where U_Id   = :Parameter.User_No
             And Lev_No = Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No
             And Nvl (Add_Flag, 0) = 1 And Rownum<=1 )))
 Order By Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No

RG_SALE_ORDR
Select   Sales_Order.So_Type, 
         Sales_Order.Order_No, 
         Sales_Order.Order_Date, 
         Sales_Order.C_Name,
         Sales_Order.A_Desc,        
         Sales_Order.Ref_Doc_No, 
         Sales_Order.Order_Ser, 
         Sales_Order.Brn_No
    From Sales_Order
   Where Sales_Order.Procesed = 0    
     And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = Sales_Order.Brn_No
                   And Nvl(Fill_Flag, 1) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1))
Order By Sales_Order.So_Type, Sales_Order.Order_No

RG_SALES_ORDR
SELECT   SO_TYPE,
         ORDER_NO,
         ORDER_DATE,
         C_Code,
         C_NAME,
         ORDER_CUR,
         DECODE (PROCESED,
                 1, IAS_GEN_PKG.GET_PROMPT (:PARAMETER.LANG_NO, 723),
                 IAS_GEN_PKG.GET_PROMPT (:PARAMETER.LANG_NO, 724)
                ) US,
         ORDER_SER,
         BRN_NO
    FROM SALES_ORDER
   WHERE nvl(PROCESED,0)=0
  And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = Sales_Order.Brn_No
                   And Nvl(Fill_Flag, 1) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1))
ORDER BY ORDER_DATE DESC, ORDER_NO DESC,SO_TYPE

RG_ALT_ITM
Select   A.I_Code_Altntv I_CODE,  
         Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,1,Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name),Nvl(M.I_E_Name,M.I_Name)) I_Name,  
         A.Itm_Unt_Altntv ITM_UNT,
         Decode(:Parameter.User_No,1,
                 Get_Icode_Avlqty (A.I_Code_Altntv,D.P_Size,Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.W_Code,:Ias_Pos_Bill_DTL.W_Code)),
                 Get_Icode_Avlqty_Priv (A.I_Code_Altntv, D.P_Size,Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.W_Code,:Ias_Pos_Bill_DTL.W_Code),
                 :Parameter.User_No)) Avl_Qty, 
         P.I_Price I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Group_No,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D,Ias_Itm_Altrntv A,Ias_Item_Price P
    Where A.I_Code=:ORDER_DETAIL.I_Code
     And M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And A.I_Code_Altntv=M.I_Code
     And A.I_Code_Altntv=D.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
     And Nvl(D.No_Sale,0) = 0    
     And A.I_Code_Altntv=P.I_Code(+)
     And A.Itm_Unt_Altntv=P.Itm_Unt(+)
     And P.Lev_No(+) =:Parameter.Price_Level
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists (Select 1
                 From Privilege_Gc
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And G_Code = M.G_Code
                   And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1))   
Order By A.Ordr_No

SELECT C_GROUP_CODE,C_CLASS,C_DEGREE,C_CLASS_TYP   FROM CUSTOMER  WHERE C_CODE = :b1  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT WHG_CODE   FROM WAREHOUSE_DETAILS  WHERE W_CODE = :b1"SELECT M.SC_NO,M.SC_NAME,M.CALC_TYPE,NVL(M.SC_TYPE,1) SC_TYPE,NVL(M.AMT_TYPE,0) AMT_TYP2,NVL(M.AMT_TYP_VAL,0),CLC_VAT_OTHR_TYP,DECODE(M.AMT_TYPE,1,DECODE(M.A_CY,:b1,M.AMT,M.AMT * M.AC_RATE  * 1  / :b2 ), NULL ) AMT,DECODE(M.AMT_TYPE,0,M.AMT, NULL ) AMT_PER,M.SC_SI_TYPE,M.SC_CST_TYPE,M.SC_WCODE_TYPE,M.A_CODE_OTHR,M.AC_CODE_DTL_OTHR,M.AC_DTL_TYP_OTHR,ALLW_MOD_A_CODE_OTHR,M.A_CY,M.AC_RATE,NVL(M.OTHR_ACCNT_CST_ACCNT_FLG,0) OTHR_ACCNT_CST_ACCNT_FLG,M.CC_CODE,M.PJ_NO,M.ACTV_NO   FROM SALES_CHARGES M  WHERE NVL(M.FILL_AUTO,0) = 1  AND NVL(M.USE_IN_POS_FLG,0) = 1  AND NVL(M.INV_ITEM,0) = 0  AND NVL(M.SC_ADD_FRC_INVOICE,0) = 0  AND NVL(M.DIFF_CMPNS_QTY_SR,0) = 0  AND NVL(INACTIVE,0) = 0  AND NVL(SC_TYPE,0) != 3 ORDER BY M.SC_NO"SELECT M.SC_NAME,M.A_CODE,M.AC_CODE_DTL,M.AC_DTL_TYP,DECODE(M.AMT_TYPE,1,M.AMT, NULL ) AMT,DECODE(M.AMT_TYPE,0,M.AMT, NULL ) AMT_PER,M.CALC_TYPE,NVL(M.SC_TYPE,1) SC_TYPE,M.A_CODE_OTHR,M.AC_CODE_DTL_OTHR,M.AC_DTL_TYP_OTHR   FROM SALES_CHARGES M  WHERE NVL(M.AMT_TYPE,0) = 0  AND NVL(M.USE_IN_POS_FLG,0) = 1  AND NVL(M.FILL_AUTO,0) = 1  AND NVL(M.INV_ITEM,0) = 0  AND NVL(M.SC_ADD_FRC_INVOICE,0) = 0  AND NVL(M.DIFF_CMPNS_QTY_SR,0) = 0  AND NVL(INACTIVE,0) = 0  AND NVL(M.BILL_DOC_TYPE,0) = DECODE(NVL(BILL_DOC_TYPE,0),0,0,NVL(:b1,0)) ORDER BY CALC_TYPE"UPDATE ORDER_DETAIL SET OTHR_AMT=0,VAT_AMT_OTHR=0 WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1"SELECT NVL(ORDER_AMT,0),NVL(ORDER_AMT,0) - NVL(DISC_AMT_DTL,0)    FROM SALES_ORDER  WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT 1   FROM ORDER_DETAIL  WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1  AND I_QTY > 0  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT SUM(NVL(FREE_QTY,0) * NVL(I_PRICE,0) )   FROM ORDER_DETAIL  WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1"SELECT 1   FROM POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE DOC_SRL = :b1  AND DOC_TYPE = 149  AND ROWNUM <= 1"UPDATE ORDER_DETAIL A SET OTHR_AMT=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(A.OTHR_AMT,0) + (SUM(NVL(POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.AMT,0)) / NVL(:b1,0) ) * NVL(A.I_PRICE,0)  ,9)   FROM POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.DOC_SRL = A.ORDER_SER  AND DOC_TYPE = 149  AND POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.DOC_SRL = :b2 ) WHERE ORDER_SER = :b2  AND NVL(I_QTY,0) > 0"UPDATE ORDER_DETAIL A SET OTHR_AMT=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(A.OTHR_AMT,0) + (SUM(NVL(POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.AMT,0)) / NVL(:b1,0) ) * NVL(A.I_PRICE,0)  ,9)   FROM POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.DOC_SRL = A.ORDER_SER  AND DOC_TYPE = 149  AND POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.DOC_SRL = :b2 ) WHERE ORDER_SER = :b2"UPDATE SALES_ORDER SET OTHR_AMT=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(SUM(AMT),0),:b1)   FROM POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE DOC_TYPE = 149  AND DOC_SRL = :b2 ) WHERE ORDER_SER = :b2"UPDATE SALES_ORDER A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=(SELECT SUM(NVL(VAT_AMT,0))   FROM POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE DOC_SRL = A.ORDER_SER  AND DOC_TYPE = 149  AND DOC_SRL = :b1 ) WHERE ORDER_SER = :b2"UPDATE ORDER_DETAIL A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=(SELECT ROUND((NVL(SALES_ORDER.VAT_AMT_OTHR,0) / NVL(SALES_ORDER.ORDER_AMT,0) ) * NVL(A.I_PRICE,0) ,9)   FROM SALES_ORDER  WHERE ORDER_SER = A.ORDER_SER  AND ORDER_SER = :b1 ) WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1"UPDATE SALES_ORDER A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=0 WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1"UPDATE ORDER_DETAIL A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=0 WHERE ORDER_SER = :b1"UPDATE POS_RQ_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT A SET VAT_PRCNT=0,VAT_AMT=0 WHERE DOC_TYPE = 149  AND DOC_SRL = :b1"
